OBJECT Page 119 User Setup
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=21-03-17;
    Time=13:03:11;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=NAVW110.00,Exercise 1;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=User Setup;
    SourceTable=Table91;
    PageType=List;
    OnOpenPage=BEGIN
                 HideExternalUsers;
               END;

  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1900000001;0;Container;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 1   ;1   ;Group     ;
                GroupType=Repeater }

    { 2   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies a user ID.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="User ID" }

    { 1000000000;2;Field  ;
                SourceExpr="Example Enabled" }

    { 4   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the earliest date on which the user is allowed to post to the company.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Allow Posting From" }

    { 6   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the last date on which the user is allowed to post to the company.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Allow Posting To" }

    { 8   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies whether to register the user's time usage defined as the time spent from when the user logs in to when the user logs out.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Register Time" }

    { 5   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the code for the salesperson or purchaser for the user.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Salespers./Purch. Code" }

    { 15  ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the code for the responsibility center to which you want to assign the user.;

OBJECT Page 50001 Sales per Customer
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=29-09-15;
    Time=15:13:39;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=Exercise 4;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    SourceTable=Table50001;
    PageType=List;
    SourceTableTemporary=Yes;
    OnOpenPage=BEGIN
                 InitPageBasedOnQuery;
               END;

  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1   ;0   ;Container ;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 2   ;1   ;Group     ;
                Name=Group;
                GroupType=Repeater }

    { 3   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer No." }

    { 4   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer Name" }

    { 5   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer City" }

    { 6   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Item No." }

    { 7   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Valued Qty." }

    { 8   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Sales Amount (Actual)" }

    { 9   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Item Description" }

  }
  CODE
  {

    PROCEDURE InitPageBasedOnQuery@1();
    VAR
      ExQuery@1002 : Query 50000;
      NextEntryNo@1001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      ExQuery.OPEN;
      WHILE ExQuery.READ DO BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := NextEntryNo + 1;
        "Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
        "Customer No." := ExQuery.No;
        "Customer Name" := ExQuery.Name;
        "Customer City" := ExQuery.City;
        "Item No." := ExQuery.Item_No;
        "Valued Qty." := ExQuery.Sum_Valued_Quantity;
        "Sales Amount (Actual)" := ExQuery.Sum_Sales_Amount_Actual;
        "Item Description" := ExQuery.Description;
        INSERT;
      END;

      FINDFIRST;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

                Visible=FALSE;
                PartType=System;
                SystemPartID=Notes }

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      ReportPrint@1000 : Codeunit 228;
      ExJnlMgt@1001 : Codeunit 50010;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DataCaption@1() : Text[250];
    VAR
      ResJnlTemplate@1000 : Record 50012;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT CurrPage.LOOKUPMODE THEN
        IF GETFILTER("Journal Template Name") <> '' THEN
          IF GETRANGEMIN("Journal Template Name") = GETRANGEMAX("Journal Template Name") THEN
            IF ResJnlTemplate.GET(GETRANGEMIN("Journal Template Name")) THEN
              EXIT(ResJnlTemplate.Name + ' ' + ResJnlTemplate.Description);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}
